     <h1>
      Men's Tees
     </h1>
    </div>
    <div class="clear">
    </div>
    <div class="desktop-12 mobile-3" id="full-width-filter">
     <ul id="sortme">
      <li class="clearfix filter">
       <p>
        Color
       </p>
       <select class="styled-select coll-filter">
        <option value="">
         All
        </option>

      /* Product Tag Filters - Good for any number of filters on any type of collection pages */
    /* Give you product tag filter select element a class of coll-filter */
    /* Give your collection select a class of coll-picker */
    /* Brought to you by Caroline Schnapp */
    var allFilters = jQuery('.coll-filter, .coll-picker');

    allFilters.change(function() {
      var newTags = [];
      var size_q = jQuery('#size-filter option:selected').text();
      
      jQuery('.coll-filter').each(function() { 
        if (jQuery(this).val()) {
          newTags.push(jQuery(this).val());
        }
      });
      if (newTags.length) {
        var query = newTags.join('+');
        if (jQuery('.coll-picker').length) {
          window.location.href = '/collections/' + jQuery('.coll-picker').val() + '/' + query + (size_q.length ? ('?size=' + size_q) : '');
        }
        else {
          window.location.href = jQuery('&lt;a title="Show products matching tag tag" href="/collections/mens-tees/tag"&gt;tag&lt;/a&gt;').attr('href').replace('tag', query) + (size_q.length ? ('?size=' + size_q) : '');
        }
      } 
      else {
        if (jQuery('.coll-picker').length) {
          window.location.href = '/collections/' + jQuery('.coll-picker').val() + (size_q.length ? ('?size=' + size_q) : '');
        }
        else {
          
          window.location.href = '/collections/mens-tees' + (size_q.length ? ('?size=' + size_q) : '');
          
        }
      }
    });
     </script>

     <div id="product-loop">
      <script>
       var products_json = [];
      
function buyx_product_json(product) {
     var variants = []
     //does it have BuyXDiscount option?
     var option_position = -1
     for (var oi = 0, olen = product.options.length; oi &lt; olen; oi++) {
         if (product.options[oi] == "BuyXDiscount") {
             option_position = oi+1
             break
         }
     }
     if (option_position == -1) {
         return product
     }
     if (product.options.length &gt; 1) {
          product.options.splice(option_position-1, 1)
     } else {
          product.options[0] = "Title"
     }
     option_position = "option" + option_position
     product.available = false
     for (var vi = 0, vlen = product.variants.length; vi &lt; vlen; vi++) {
         if (product.variants[vi][option_position] == "Default") {
             product.variants[vi][option_position] = ""
             variants.push(product.variants[vi])
             product.available = product.available || product.variants[vi].available
         }
     }
     product.variants = variants
     return product
  }
      </script>

    <script>
     // Three Column Collection Masonry
/*
  $(window).load(function () {
    var columns = 4,
        setColumns = function () {
          columns = $(window).width() &gt; 740 ? 4 : $(window).width() &gt; 500 ? 2 : 1;
        };
    
    setColumns();
    $(window).resize(setColumns);
    
    var $container = $('#content');
    $container.imagesLoaded( function() {    
      
      $('#product-loop').masonry({
        itemSelector: '.product-index',
        columnWidth: function (containerWidth) {
          return containerWidth / columns;
        },
        isAnimated: true,
        animationOptions: {
          duration: 150,
          easing: 'linear',
          queue: false
        }
      });
      
    });
    
  });
*/

  var isMobile = { 
    Android: function() { return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i); }, 
    BlackBerry: function() { return navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i); }, 
    iOS: function() { return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i); }, 
    Opera: function() { return navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i); }, 
    Windows: function() { return navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i); }, 
    any: function() { 
      return (isMobile.Android() || isMobile.BlackBerry() || isMobile.iOS() || isMobile.Opera() || isMobile.Windows()); 
    } 
  };
	
	if(!isMobile.any()){
	  $('.product-item-top').on({
	    mouseenter: function(){
	      var $me = $(this);
	      if ($me.find('.hidden-image').length) {
  	      $me
  	        .find('.initial-image').hide()
  	        .end()
  	        .find('.hidden-image').addClass('show-pic');
	      }
	    },
	    mouseleave: function(){
	      var $me = $(this);
	      if ($me.find('.hidden-image').length) {
  	      $me
  	        .find('.initial-image').show()
  	        .end()
            .find('.hidden-image').removeClass('show-pic');
        }
	    }
	  });
  }
    </script>
